    SELECT [u].[Id], [u].[Address], [u].[CompanyId], [u].[CreateDate], [u].[DateOfBirth], [u].[DeletedDate], [u].[Email], [u].[FullName], [u].[IsDeleted], [u].[IsMale], [u].[LastModifyDate], [u].[PassWordHash], [u].[PermissionId], [u].[PhoneNumber], [u].[UserName]
    FROM [User] AS [u]
    WHERE [u].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
ORDER BY [t].[LastModifyDate] DESC
